## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

The portrait of the person is on the left, the text on the right. The text occupies two-thirds of the image and the portrait one-third, with a slight gradient transition effect on the portrait.

### No. 2: Premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

Create an Infographics with bento grid 8 module layout, user can specify any product name in Food, Medicine, tech etc category, choose language, Background style, Hero grid style

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Input Variable: [insert product name]
Language: [insert language]

System Instruction:
Create an image of premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules (card 2 to 8 show text titles only).
1) Product Analysis:
â†’ Identify product's dominant natural color â†’ "hero color"
â†’ Identify category: FOOD / MEDICINE / TECH
2) Color Palette (derived from hero):
â†’ Product + accents: full saturation hero color
â†’ Icons, borders: muted hero (30-40% saturation, never black)
3) Visual Style:
â†’ Hero product: real photography (authentic, premium), 3D Glass version [choose one]
â†’ Cards: Apple liquid glass (85-90% transparent) with Whisper-thin borders and Subtle drop shadow for floating depth and reflecting the background color
â†’ Background stays behind cards and high blur where cards are [choose one]:
  - Ethereal: product essence, light caustics, abstract glow
  - Macro: product texture close-up, heavily blurred
  - Pattern: product repeated softly at 10-15% opacity
  - Context: relevant environment, blurred + desaturated
â†’ Add subtle motion effect
â†’ Asymmetric Bento grid, 16:9 landscape
â†’ Hero card: 28-30% | Info modules: 70-72%
4) Module Content (8 Cards):
M1 â€” Hero: Product displayed as real photo / 3D glass / stylized interpretation (choose one)in beautiful form + product name label
M2 â€” Core Benefits: 4 unique benefits + hero-color icons
M3 â€” How to Use: 4 usage methods + icons
M4 â€” Key Metrics: 5 EXACT data points
Format: [icon] [Label] [Bold Value] [Unit]
FOOD: Calories: [X] kcal/100g, Carbs: [X]g (fiber [X]g, sugar [X]g), Protein: [X]g, [Key Vitamin]: [X]mg ([X]% DV), [Key Mineral]: [X]mg ([X]% DV)
MEDICINE:Active: [name], Strength: [X] mg, Onset: [X] min, Duration: [X] hrs, Half-life: [X] hrs 
TECH:Chip: [model], Battery: [X] hrs, Weight: [X]g,[Key spec]: [value], Connectivity: [protocols]
M5 â€” Who It's For: 4 recommended groups with green checkmark icons | 3 caution groups with amber warning icons
M6 â€” Important Notes: 4 precautions + warning icons
M7 â€” Quick Reference:
â†’ FOOD: Glycemic Index + dietary tags with icons
â†’ MEDICINE: Side effects + severity with icons
â†’ TECH: Compatibility + certifications with icons
M8 â€” Did You Know: 3 facts (origin, science, global stat) + icons
Output: 1 image, 16:9 landscape, ultra-premium liquid glass infographic.
```

### No. 5: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

### No. 6: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

### No. 8: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 9: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

### No. 30: Social Media Post - Detailed Mirror Selfie Prompt with ControlNet Constraints

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured prompt designed for image generation, specifying the subject (young woman in specific attire and pose), environment (bedroom mirror selfie), camera perspective, lighting, mood, and style (candid, high physical realism). Crucially, it includes extensive ControlNet parameters (OpenPose and Depth) with strict constraints to lock the skeletal alignment, anatomical proportions, and volumetric projection, while using a long negative prompt to avoid stylization and artificial enhancements.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
"subject": "Young woman, long blonde hair with face-framing highlights. Wearing tight white tank top showing distinct chest volume and fabric tension, grey flared trousers, black belt with silver buckle, and black strappy high heels. Gold bracelet on left wrist. Holding a dark green smartphone with three lenses.",
"pose": "Crouching sideways, back arched. Torso twisted towards camera mirror. Right hand holds phone at face level. Left arm rests lightly on left thigh. Full body weight distributed on toes and heels.",
"environment": "Bedroom interior. White unmade bed with pillows behind subject. White textured rug on dark wood floor. White walls. Vertical window blinds visible on the left.",
"camera": "Mirror selfie perspective. Standard smartphone wide lens. Eye-level framing capturing full crouching figure.",
"lighting": "Soft natural daylight from left window. Natural soft shadows cast to the right. High-key overall illumination.",
"mood_and_expression": "Neutral expression, relaxed demeanor, direct gaze into phone mirror.",
"style_and_realism": "Candid mirror selfie photograph. High physical realism, unmodified amateur style.",
"colors_and_tone": "Neutral high-key palette. Dominant whites, greys, and blacks. Natural skin tones and blonde hair. Dark green accent from phone.",
"quality_and_technical_details": "Sharp focus smartphone image. Visible natural textures on bed sheets, ribbed tank top, and rug.",
"aspect_ratio_and_output": "3:4",
"controlnet": {
"pose_control": {
"model_type": "openpose_full",
"purpose": "Strictly lock skeletal alignment, anatomical proportions, torso orientation, and prevent structural or volumetric alteration",
"constraints": "No limb length adjustment, no torso compression, no chest volume reduction, no posture change, no symmetry correction, no ribcage narrowing",
"recommended_weight": 1.2
},
"depth_control": {
"model_type": "depth_midas",
"purpose": "Enforce exact volumetric projection, silhouette area equivalence, curvature depth integrity, and spatial layering",
"constraints": "No depth flattening, no volumetric shrinkage, no perspective reinterpretation, no shadow softening, no foreground-background collapse, no artificial depth of field",
"recommended_weight": 1.25
}
},
"negative_prompt": "stylization, cinematic look, cinematic lighting, cinematic color grading, film look, film simulation, dramatic lighting, HDR effect, tonal remapping, teal and orange grading, DSLR simulation, portrait mode effect, bokeh, background blur, depth of field, lens blur, gaussian blur, soft focus, motion blur, atmospheric haze, volumetric light beams, glow effect, bloom, post-processing effects, AI enhancement, detail enhancement filters, artificial sharpening, oversharpening, skin smoothing, retouching, face enhancement, aesthetic correction, body normalization, shape refinement, geometric reinterpretation, anatomical distortion, breast reduction, volume compression, torso slimming, ribcage narrowing, sym"
```

### No. 39: Infographic / Edu Visual - Technical Infographic Overlay for Object Annotation

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured prompt template designed to generate an infographic image by combining a realistic photograph of an object with an overlay of technical, architectural-style annotations. It specifies using only black lines on a white background for labels, internal outlines, measurements, and functional arrows, creating an educational, engineering manual aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Create an infographic image of {argument name="object" default="[OBJECT]"}, combining a realistic photograph or photorealistic rendering of the object with an overlay of technical annotations placed directly on top.
Use black ink line drawings and text (in the style of a technical pen / architectural sketch) on a clean white studio background, including:
â€¢ Labels on key components
â€¢ Internal outlines in cutaway or cross-section view
â€¢ Measurement, dimension, and scale markers
â€¢ Material and quantity designations
â€¢ Arrows indicating function, force, or flow (air, sound, power, pressure)
â€¢ Simple diagrams or cross-sections where appropriate

Style and layout rules:
â€¢ The real object remains clearly visible under the annotations
â€¢ Annotations look schematic, technical, and architectural
â€¢ Clear composition with balanced negative space
â€¢ Educational atmosphere resembling a museum exhibition or engineering manual.
Visual style:
Minimalist technical illustration aesthetics, black lines over realistic images, crisp but slightly hand-drawn.
Color palette:
White background, only black annotation lines and text. No colors.
Output:
1080x1080 resolution, very sharp image, optimized for social media, no watermarks.
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a 2x3 grid of cinematic film stills capturing an intimate home dance sequence. The prompt specifies complex parameters including image-to-image mode, preservation of identity and pose, specific lighting (warm soft ambient), camera settings (35mm, f/2.0), and detailed subject wardrobe (deep red satin dress) and motion blur control.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "task_type": "home_dance_film_still_grid_2x3_red_satin",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.0_HOME_DANCE_2X3_RED_SATIN_FILM"
    },
    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "very_high",
      "preserve_identity": true,
      "preserve_facial_features": true,
      "preserve_pose_dynamics": true,
      "notes": "Use the reference collage as the primary anchor. Keep the same couple, same room, same framing and dance flow across six panels. Change the woman's dress to a deep red satin dress with elegant sheen. Maintain realistic motion blur from dancing while keeping faces readable."
    },
    "output": {
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
      "resolution": "ultra_high",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 2,
        "cols": 3,
        "gutter": "thin",
        "panel_consistency": "high"
      },
      "sharpness": "filmic_soft",
      "grain": "subtle_analog",
      "halation": "soft"
    },
    "scene": {
      "concept": "intimate home dance sequence captured as cinematic film stills",
      "environment": "cozy interior hallway/living room, simple door and framed picture on wall, warm daylight or tungsten mix",
      "lighting": {
        "style": "warm soft ambient light",
        "key_light": "window-like soft side light",
        "fill_light": "gentle fill to keep skin detail",
        "shadow_behavior": "soft, slightly hazy",
        "avoid": "hard flash, harsh HDR"
      }
    },
    "camera": {
      "lens": "35mm",
      "aperture": "f/2.0",
      "depth_of_field": "shallow to medium",
      "look": "vintage film still, slight softness and bloom"
    },
    "subjects": {
      "count": 2,
      "type": "adult couple",
      "male": {
        "wardrobe": "white fitted t-shirt, dark trousers",
        "notes": "keep outfit simple and consistent across panels"
      },
      "female": {
        "wardrobe": {
          "dress": "deep red satin midi dress, elegant drape, fluid skirt, subtle sheen highlights, fitted bodice",
          "details": "satin fabric reflections should look realistic and soft, not metallic"
        },
        "hair": "short bob haircut (keep consistent with reference if visible)"
      },
      "anatomy_rules": "correct hands and fingers, natural grip during dance, realistic arm alignment"
    },
    "motion_style": {
      "dance_energy": "gentle but dynamic",
      "blur": "controlled motion blur on dress and arms during spins, faces remain mostly readable",
      "camera_motion": "static camera, movement comes from subjects"
    },
    "grid_plan": {
      "panel_1": "couple starting to dance, close playful steps near the door",
      "panel_2": "facing each other holding hands, smiling, preparing to spin",
      "panel_3": "man dips woman slightly, red satin skirt flowing",
      "panel_4": "wo

  }
}
```

### No. 65: Comic / Storyboard - Manga Evolution Architectural Section Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured prompt designed to generate an image depicting the 'Evolution of Manga' as a detailed architectural section, showing four stacked strata representing different phases, complete with representative artifacts and educational transitions, rendered with architectural realism.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Evolution of Manga --> <LAYOUT> A single chunky block (like a museum cutaway) sliced to reveal 4 stacked floors/strata. Each level represents an era/stage/version inferred from INPUT. Right side: a vertical legend bar with dates/period labels inferred by the model. </LAYOUT>
<INFER_AND_RENDER> Infer 4 major phases and depict each with representative artifacts, tools, and environments. Keep transitions educational: show what changed between levels (materials, scale, method). </INFER_AND_RENDER>
<STYLE_NOTES> Architectural section realism: visible thickness, rebar/fasteners if applicable, realistic debris at cut edge. </STYLE_NOTES>
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

### No. 69: Comic / Storyboard - Morning Routine Video Generation using Kling 3.0

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed video prompt generated by Freepik's assistant (GPT-5) based on an image from Nano Banana Pro, used to create a short film sequence with Kling 3.0. The prompt outlines three scenes focusing on smooth camera movements, close-ups of morning rituals, and a cinematic conclusion.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Scene 1
Use a smooth dolly shot to approach the window, transitioning from a long shot to a medium shot of the subject taking a deep breath in the morning light. Focus on subtle movements like relaxing the shoulders and finger reactions, creating an adorable atmosphere with distant natural sounds (birds chirping, wind) layered with delicate piano music. Crossfade to a close-up where the window light reflects on the fingertips.

Scene 2
Use close-ups focusing on steaming cups and small objects to rhythmically follow the hand movements (lifting the cup, stirring with a spoon, etc.). Use a combination of slow motion and light time-lapse to express warmth and innocence, layering sound effects like breathing and small laughs. The steam fills the screen and dissolves, leading to the next scene.

Scene 3
The camera pulls back to show the whole scene, concluding with the light movement of the subject ready to go out. Show the lingering atmosphere through the rhythm of steps and hand gestures, concluding cinematically with a backlit silhouette and soft color tones. The music gently fades out, leaving the lingering feeling of everyday life.
```

### No. 76: Product Marketing - Whimsical Diorama of a Fortified Desert Caravanserai

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A comprehensive miniature diorama prompt shell for generating a fortified desert caravanserai, detailing the scene, architecture, composition, and a stylized aesthetic resembling a collectible model sculpted from matte ceramic or resin.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
MASTER MINIATURE DIORAMA PROMPT SHELL â€” CONSOLIDATED VERSION
SCENE:
A fortified desert caravanserai featuring thick outer walls, a large central courtyard, multiple merchant lodging wings, camel stables, watchtowers, arched gateways, and clustered market storage rooms.

If no scene description is provided, generate a visually interesting culturally recognizable environment or architectural location of your own choosing. Create a cohesive miniature settlement, district, or environment with multiple structures, pathways, and environmental storytelling elements arranged into a contained display composition suitable for a collectible diorama.
When generating or inventing a scene, prioritize architectural and cultural diversity and intentionally vary the environment type, building styles, historical inspiration, regional influence, and settlement purpose so each generated miniature feels visually distinct and not a repetition of common village, temple, garden, or plaza layouts.
Ensure the architecture organizes around a natural central hub so structures cluster with believable spatial gravity, forming a cohesive miniature settlement with denser core structures and supporting elements arranged outward. Arrange the layout as a compact, layered, interconnected district filling the platform naturally without empty gaps. Ensure the entire environment clearly reads as a small handcrafted tabletop collectible model, with miniature-scale architecture and compressed model-world proportions rather than life-sized buildings.
STYLE:
Frame the camera at a stable product-display distance so the entire collectible diorama remains clearly visible with comfortable margins, avoiding close cinematic crops or environmental perspective shots. Render as a premium stylized 3D collectible miniature diorama on a fully visible, centered self-contained display base, shown from a slightly elevated 3/4 tabletop angle against a clean neutral studio gradient background. Maintain collectible figurine scale and clean display presentation.
All elements should appear sculpted from smooth matte ceramic, painted resin, or stylized polymer with rounded edges, simplified geometry, and slightly exaggerated toy-like proportions. Keep surfaces clean and intentionally stylized. Avoid fingerprints, rough handmade textures, workshop scenes, macro photography depth-of-field, or photoreal clay imperfections.
Use soft professional studio product lighting: gentle global illumination, warm key light, soft ambient bounce, controlled shadows, and optional warm interior window glow.
Render any water or translucent materials as poured clear resin with smooth transparency, subtle reflections, soft internal depth, and slightly thick stylized edges.
Include small environmental details but keep everything cohesive, simplified, and sculptural. Prioritize clean stylized modeling over photorealistic texture detail.
Over
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed template prompt for generating a high-fashion editorial typography poster with a strict 1:2 composition split. The prompt defines the layout, requiring a massive vertical word (acting as a stencil mask) on the left third, revealing the subject, and specific text placement and font styles (Helvetica Condensed) for a clean, graphic design aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Style & Composition: High-fashion editorial typography poster with a strict 1:2 composition split. Layout & Ratio: The frame is divided so that the right two-thirds show the full subject and background, while the left one-third is reserved for the typography masking section.

Typography Masking: A massive, ultra-bold, vertical word "[{argument name="word" default="WORD"}]" is placed on the left third. The text is strictly full-bleed, stretching perfectly and touching the absolute top and absolute bottom edges of the frame with zero vertical padding, gaps, or margins. This typography acts as a stencil mask: the letters reveal the underlying character, while the space to the far left of the letters is a solid, clean white.

Subject Details & Positioning: An upper-body shot of [{argument name="character description" default="CHARACTER DESCRIPTION"}]. The model is positioned so that only her left-most side is visible through the letters, while the rest of her body is fully visible and contained on the right side against a solid [{argument name="color" default="COLOR"}] background, ensuring no part of the subject is cropped by the right edge of the frame. Pose: [POSE DESCRIPTION], ensuring the silhouette remains within the center of the right two-thirds area.

Secondary Text: In the top right corner, add the text: "[TEXT]". Use a small, sophisticated, white "Helvetica Condensed" style font with wide letter spacing (kerning) for a premium, minimalist look. Color Palette: A strict monochromatic [COLOR] theme, sharply contrasted by the crisp white negative space on the left. 8k resolution, photorealistic textures, sharp studio lighting, high contrast, clean graphic design aesthetic.
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
ORNATE BOX DIORAMA â€” TRI-LAYER MASTER PROMPT (HARD FRONT-RIGHT ISOMETRIC)

DIORAMA_LIGHTING =
========================
LAYER 1 â€” PHYSICAL GEOMETRY (HIGHEST PRIORITY)
The ornate antique box is a solid rigid container transformed into architecture.
If BOX_VARIABLE is specified, the entire container and its carved architectural
structure must be made from that material.
If BOX_VARIABLE is empty, infer logically from THEME_LOCATION.
The full outer shell must remain intact on all sides.
No removed walls.
No dollhouse cutaway.
FRONT FACADE LOCK:
The FRONT SIDE must contain:
â€¢ exactly ONE centered door
â€¢ exactly TWO windows
â€¢ one window left of the door
â€¢ one window right of the door
Openings must be carved THROUGH the existing wall.
Apply DOOR_MATERIAL / WINDOW_MATERIAL / WINDOW_PANE_MATERIAL
if specified, otherwise infer logically.
Front wall must remain structurally thick and complete.
ORNAMENTAL DEPTH CONTINUITY LOCK:
All carvings must continue through wall thickness.
Frames must appear carved from the same solid material.
Interior walls share identical structural thickness.
The lid must match base width and length and be hinge-connected.
========================
LAYER 2 â€” SCENE LOGIC
Create a two-level miniature THEME_LOCATION fully integrated
into the container.
Use FLOOR_MATERIAL / STAIRCASE_TYPE / STAIRCASE_MATERIAL /
MEZZANINE_FLOOR_MATERIAL if specified, otherwise infer logically.
Upper level attaches directly to container walls.
The inside of the lid functions as the vaulted ceiling.
All props, materials, and architecture must match THEME_LOCATION.
========================
LAYER 3 â€” RENDER & CAMERA
Ultra-realistic cinematic miniature diorama photography.
Use DIORAMA_LIGHTING if specified.
========================
HARD FRONT-RIGHT ISOMETRIC CAMERA SYSTEM
CORNER ANCHOR RULE:
The FRONT-RIGHT TOP CORNER of the box must be the closest point to the viewer.
WALL VISIBILITY RATIO RULE:
The front wall must occupy slightly more visible area than the right wall.
Approximate visual dominance:
â€¢ front wall â‰ˆ 60% visibility
â€¢ right wall â‰ˆ 40% visibility
Both must be clearly visible simultaneously.
RIM OCCLUSION RULE:
Camera must remain above the front wall rim.
The top edge of the front wall must overlap a small portion of the interior floor.
Interior must be seen OVER the wall, never through a missing wall.
FORBIDDEN CAMERA POSITIONS:
Do NOT center the camera on the front wall.
Do NOT use a straight frontal view.
Do NOT use a top-down view.
Do NOT prioritize interior visibility over box geometry.
COMPOSITION TARGET:
The image must resemble a professionally photographed miniature collectible
box viewed from a stable elevated front
```

```
A stylized medieval fantasy village at morning featuring a Market Square Shopfront with timber awning frame and striped fabric canopy, a Village Inn with carved wooden balcony railings and dormer windows, a Timber-Framed Village Cottage built on a stone foundation base with exposed timber beams and plaster wall panels, a Noble Manor House with multiple steep shingled roofs and decorative roof finials, a Stone Watchtower with circular tower windows and crenellation detail, and an Arched Gatehouse with keystoned arch and portcullis gate. Artisan stalls are arranged in structured rows across the cobblestone square with clear walking lanes between them. Potters, weavers, and woodcarvers display goods beneath striped canopies while villagers gather in moderate evenly spaced clusters. Guards maintain presence near the gatehouse and market edges. The Reflective Water Body remains unobstructed and calm, with activity confined to dock platforms only. Dense pine forest clusters and rounded shrubs frame the vibrant yet orderly craft fair.

Style:
Cinematic stylized fantasy medieval village, warm golden morning sunlight, long soft shadows, clean blue sky illumination, subtle volumetric light rays, painterly materials, softened stone and wood textures, vibrant but controlled color grading, rounded stylized forms, balanced exposure, atmospheric clarity, cozy environmental realism, high-end game environment quality
```

### No. 116: Game Asset - Batgirl Bodysuit Portrait with Likeness Preservation Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific, JSON-formatted prompt for generating a photorealistic portrait of a woman in a Batgirl-inspired bodysuit, emphasizing the preservation of the reference image's exact facial structure, body proportions, and skin texture, while detailing the outfit and environment.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "subject": {
    "desc": "Use the exact character from the provided reference image, preserving her unique facial structure, skin tone, hairstyle, eye color, proportions, and overall likeness. Tiny Batgirl-style mask covering eyes.",
    "apparel": {
      "item": "Batgirl inspired bodysuit",
      "style": "Halter-neck sleeveless, high-cut legs",
      "color": "Black base with glossy purple accents, yellow trim on legs, large yellow bat emblem on chest",
      "details": "Tight stretch fabric emphasizing curves, black/purple stockings"
    },
    "anatomy": {
      "body_type": "Match the exact body proportions of the reference character without alteration",
      "bust": "Maintain the original size, volume, projection, and natural containment from the reference image",
      "hips": "Preserve the original hip width, thigh thickness, and waist ratio exactly as in the reference",
      "skin": "Replicate the natural skin texture, tone variation, and surface detail from the reference image"
    }
  },
  "pose": {
    "posture": "Standing upright, weight shifted to right hip (viewer's left) for pelvic tilt, torso slightly angled toward camera",
    "limbs": {
      "right_arm": "Extended down, hand resting on granite countertop",
      "left_arm": "Hanging naturally by side, partially obscured by hip",
      "head": "Slight tilt, facing forward"
    },
    "gaze": "Direct eye contact, soft neutral confident sultry expression"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "Indoor bathroom",
    "elements": [
      "Speckled green/black granite countertop (left foreground)",
      "Wooden door with tall frosted glass panel",
    ]
  },
  "camera": {
    "shot": "Medium (thighs up), vertical 3:4",
    "angle": "Eye-level slightly frontal",
    "lens": "50-85mm portrait",
    "dof": "Moderate depth of field, subject sharply in focus, background slightly softened but still distinct",
    "framing": "Centered subject"
  },
  "lighting": "Soft diffuse indoor artificial lighting, overhead/slightly frontal, even illumination, soft shadows under natural contours, realistic highlights on fabric sheen and skin texture",
  "mood": "Confident calm sultry, casual intimate domestic atmosphere",
  "style": "Photorealistic smartphone photography, high-fidelity detailed fabric and skin textures, natural color grading, realistic physical proportions matching reference",
  "colors": "Black suit with vibrant yellow/purple accents dominant, green/black granite, warm wood tones, neutral walls, natural contrast and saturation",
  "quality": "High-definition sharp focus on eyes/face/suit pattern, low noise, minimal grain, realistic dynamic range",
```

### No. 117: Poster / Flyer - Gallery-Quality Tribute Poster with Textured Photo Mosaic Silhouette

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex prompt for creating a high-quality tribute poster featuring a central black and white portrait silhouette filled with a dense, textured photo mosaic. The prompt emphasizes a tactile, layered, and premium aesthetic, avoiding flat digital collage work, and includes strict guidelines for color, typography, and composition.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Create a refined, gallery-quality tribute poster built around a central portrait silhouette filled with a textured photo mosaic. The design should feel tactile, layered, and premium not like flat digital collage work. 

Central Structure : The Vessel The central focus must be a large-scale, high-contrast black and white portrait silhouette of {argument name="person's name" default="[Persons name]"}.
This silhouette acts as the container for the internal visual narrative. It must be centered perfectly on the canvas. The Grid Fill and Mixed Media Textures The interior of the silhouette should be populated by a dense photo mosaic grid made from action shots throughout the personâ€™s career. Critical Texture Direction Do not paste flat photos. Each grid cell should have artistic treatment to create a tactile, collage-like aesthetic. Incorporate a mix of the following textures selectively across different cells: Halftone dots (comic-book style raster patterns) 
Fabric or embroidery textures suggesting jersey material or stitched patches Film grain or heavy noise on high-contrast action shots The result should feel handcrafted and layered rather than digitally assembled. 

Color Strategy Base palette: monochrome black and white. Introduce selective color overlays only on specific grid cells. The accent colors should relate to the relevant team, brand, or national flag. Use color sparingly to create visual rhythm and emphasis. 

Typography and Branding â€“ Strict Micro-Scaling Top Left (The name) Write â€œ{argument name="person's name" default="[person name]"}â€ using the font Inter Semibold. Kerning: tight negative kerning , Size: small and discreet. The name must occupy a maximum of 20% of the total canvas width. Do not make it large or dominant. 
Top Right (The symbol) Place the primary logo (Team, Brand, or Flag). Size: very small. It must occupy a maximum of 10% of the total canvas width. 

Composition and Background Background Use off-white or light grey. Include a visible high-quality paper or subtle concrete texture. Avoid flat digital white. 
Alignment Center the silhouette precisely. Maintain generous negative space around the figure to preserve elegance and balance.
```

This shot is processed with the Valencia Instagram filter for a warm, vintage-inspired pop, layered over a Kodak Portra 400 LUT for creamy skin tones and muted highlights. The composition feels candid and human, with a slight amateur off-center crop that gives it a raw, front-row fan-captured energy, featuring realistic lens flare blooming in the upper left corner and fine film grain throughout. ## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
